Changed files:

		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/CmdExtrude.cpp?rev=1.5.6.4
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/CmdRegion.cpp?rev=1.5.6.4
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/CmdRevolve.cpp?rev=1.5.6.6
		Source/prj/ICAD/IcadUtil.h?rev=1.1.4.2
                Source/prj/make/icad.dsw?rev=1.6.6.2
                Source/prj/ICAD/res/icadrc2.h?rev=1.59.4.19
		Eng-us/icad.rc2?rev=1.63.4.26

Description:	This submission reimplemented the REGION command and made some major
                changes to the EXTRUDE and REVOLVE commands in order to fix the bug 
                #78522 - "Boolean operations not possible with region and extruded 
                entities" and following REGION, XTRUDE, and REVOLVE problems, which 
                are not reported: 
		
		1) The separated, non-overlapping regions were created by REGION 
		   command for the intersected curves(i.e. REGION incorrectly created 
		   3 separated, non overlapping regions for two intersected circles), 
		   which is wrong totally. 
		
		2) In the certain cases, the resions created had wrong normal face 
		   direction, which caused EXTRUDE and REVOLVE to create invalid solid 
		   with negative volumn or sweep face along wrong direction.
		
		3) All selected curves were deleted after the regions were created when 
		   some of them were rejected because they don't belong to any loop.
		   
		4) The selected curves were not unhighlighted when REGION, EXTRUDE, and 
		   REVOLVE commands failed.
		
		5) No error messages were given when REGION, EXTRUDE, and REVOLVE  
		   commands failed.
		
		6) Unable to create extruded solids with a taper angle.
		
		The original implemtation of REGION did not consider the input curves 
		could be either open or closed, and form some loops that may intersect 
		each other. It just simply passed all selected curves to ACIS modeler 
		to create regions, which is wrong and caused some of problems above.
		The new implemtation build the loops from the curves first and then
		test them to reject non-planar or/and self-intersected loops. The 
		manifold vertex case is also taken acocunt. The double side regions 
		are created from the loops.
		
Comments:	TaL78522

Date:		04-30-2003
Developer:	Stephen Hou
Company:	Nd Space
Reference:	BugZilla:78470

Changed files: 	
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/CmdFilletChamfer.cpp?rev=1.1.2.7 
		Source/prj/ICAD/res/icadrc2.h?rev=1.59.4.16
		Eng-us/icad.rc2?rev=1.63.4.24

Description:	This submission fixed polyline fillet and chamfer problem
                reported in #78470 and other polyline releated problems 
                memtioned at below, which have not been reported.
                
		1) FILLET/CHAMFER incorectly allowed the selected lines to 
		   be seaprated by more than one polyline segment.

		2) They incorrectly filleted and chamfered all vertices 
		   between selected edges.

		3) For the case the lines are separated by one polyline segment, 
		   they didn't replace the segment with fillet a chamfer line 
		   or fillet.

		4) For the closed polylines, which vertex would be chamfered 
		   or filleted was incorrectly depending on the selected order.
Comments:       TaL78470

AFFECTED FILES:	
	
	Source/prj/lib/DB/Modeler.h?rev=1.9.6.5

	Source/prj/lib/CMDS/CmdRevolve.cpp?rev=1.5.6.5	
	Source/prj/lib/CMDS/cmds8.cpp?rev=1.15.6.9
	Source/prj/lib/CMDS/CmdQueryTools.cpp?rev=1.5.6.6
	Source/prj/lib/CMDS/CmdSolidedit.inl?rev=1.3.6.3
	Source/prj/lib/CMDS/CmdSolidedit.h?rev=1.4.6.3
	Source/prj/lib/CMDS/CmdSolidedit.cpp?rev=1.5.6.4

DESCRIPTIONS:	
 
 	This submission made following changes to the code to fix problems:
 	
        1) Added 3D solids/bodeis support to SOLIDEDIT/Imprint to imprint the 
           intersection graph of 3D solids and bodies onto the solids/bodeis.
                
        2) Offsetting a face that was created by imprinting a circle on a 3D solid
           crashed IntelliCAD. The problem is ACIS' api_offset_faces() creates
           an invalid body in the case but doesn't return any error. This problem 
           was fixed by adding a call to api_check_entity() to verify the body after 
           calling api_offset_faces().
           
        3) Unable to change the color of faces of 3D solids. The problem was that 
           we attached the color attribute to the face entity only but not edges.
           This bug was fixed by attaching the color to the edges of the face also.
        
        4) Changed to cmd_extrude() and cmd_revolve() to delete temporary curves 
           created by geodata::extract() to create regions.
           
        5) Modified cmd_subtract() to fix display problem.
        
        6) Modified CCmdQueryEntity::query() to ask users to select an entity
           again if the picked point was not on any entity. Originally the
           function was implemented to throw an exception if the users clicked a 
           point that was not on the wireframe of any entity, which caused the command
           to be terminated. Also modified this function to highlight the selected
           entity.
           
	7) Fixed SOLIDEDIT that was not able to change face color.
	
	8) Modified SOLIDEDIT to prevent terminating the command in the case when 
	   the modeler failed to performance local operation. 
	   
	9) The face editing subcommands, Extrude and Offset in SOLIDEDIT did remove
	   selected face form the screen. Those problems have been fixed.

File Name:	VS_28022003_1.txt
Date:		28-02-2003
Developer:	Vittalbabu Srinivasan
Company:	Mantra Software
Reference:	

Changed files: 	
		Source/prj/lib/GR/2D.CPP?rev=1.1.4.1.2.2
		Source/prj/lib/GR/coordconvert.CPP?rev=1.7.8.2

Description:	This submission fixes an infinite loop in the display code and merges one change from R40_dev to R40_from_11.
Comments:	In this submission the following change from R40_Dev is merged into R40_from_11. Also fixed an infinite loop
		in gr_clip_vector().

		In gr_clip_vector() the input is a clip rectangle and 4 values represnting the 2 end points of the line
		to be clipped. It is possible that the data for a line segment being clipped could have invalid values (QNAN).
		An example of how this can be generated is when user creates a line, and invokes F8 when a point is
		requested. The presence of a NAN makes the gr_clip_vector() go into an infinite loop. The fix was to have a
		counter which keeps track of the number of times the input line segment is clipped against the window. If the
		counter reaches 5, the loop exits and returns 1 (to signify the line was outside the clip rectangle). In the normal
		case, we can clip a line max. of 4 times against the clip rectange.

		Date:		28-02-2003
		Developer:	DenisPetrov
		Company:	ITC
		Affected files:	
			Source/prj/lib/GR/2D.CPP 
		Description:	Fixed method of rect class for checking intersections.

		Source/prj/make/icad.dsp

Added files:	Source/prj/ICAD/DlgSpoolingSettings.cpp,
		Source/prj/ICAD/DlgSpoolingSettings.h
Description:	
		1.Implemented intersession storing of Printer Setup dialog settings:
		printer name, paper orientation, paper size and paper source
		(the dialog is called by PSETUP command).
		- These settings are stored in the system registry and used for
		printing and showed in the dialog when it's called.
		- If stored printer is absent in the system when it's needed
		then it's automatically overridden with system default printer
		and its settings.

		2.Implemented icad spooling features
		- the user can force print output to PRN files;
		- the user can set a folder where PRN files are stored;
		- PRN filenames are generated according to the template
		  MMDDYY_HHMMSS(_unique index when needed)_DWGNAME.PRN (if it's necessary according to settings).
		The settings of this mechanism can be changed in the
		'Spooling settings' dialog called from 'Print Setup' one ('Print Setup'
		is called by PSETUP command) and stored in the system registry.
		[This change can be undone by removing or commenting of

Date:		31-12-2002
Developer:	Stephen Hou
Company:	Nd Space
Reference:	SH_31122002.txt
Changed files:	
   		Source/prj/ICAD/icadapi.cpp?rev=1.64.4.14 
   		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/panzoom.cpp?rev=1.3.10.1 
   		Source/prj/lib/DRW/dwgload.cpp?rev=1.48.4.14 
Description:	This submission fixes the following crash bugs:
		BugZilla:78191: ICAD crashes if some text is typed at the prompt and 
		then backspace key is kept pressed

		RESOLUTION: The code didn't record how many characters users entered at the 
		command prompt and just kept to move back the file position pointer 
		when the backspace key is kept pressed until ICAD crashed. This 
		also caused the all records in the script file to be erased.
		This bug was fixed by modifying SDS_SendMessage() to use a static 
		variable in to record the number of characters users just entered 
		at the prompt and ensure the file pointer will not be moved back 
		more than the number of characters the users entered.
		
		BugZilla:78387: ICAD crashes while opening attached drawing.
             
		RESOLUTION: The drawing contains a NULL handle of ACDBVARIABLEDICTIONARY 
		dictionary item but the code didn't check the handle and directly 
		added it into dictionary that caused ICAD to cash later. To 
		fix up, some checks are added into the code to prevent NULL
		handles to be added to the dictionary. AutoCAD also does similar 
		fix up 
		
		
		BugZilla:78373: ICAD crashes for zoom>extents operation after inserting attached 
		drawing.
		
		RESOLUTION: The implantation of display object list is not thread safe. When 
		the ZOOM command is executed, the main win thread will perform tool 
		hit test on the display object list if hyperlink tooltip is enabled 
		while the command thread is updating the display object list. So
		the memory of display object list that main thread holds for test
		can be freed by the command thread sometimes before the main thread
		complete the test. That causes ICAD to crash randomly, depending on
		the thread schedule. This bug is fixed by temporarily disable the
		hyperlink tooltip at the begin of cmd_zoom().		

Comments:	Added script 78387.scr, 78373.scr.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Date:		12-12-2002
Developer:	DenisPetrov
Company:	ITC
Reference:	
Description:	Introducing checking of drawing loading phase. The purpose is 
		to provide uniform approach to checking and validating incorrect 
		drawing elements. It is necessary to give ability to load different 
		corrupted drawings.
		After drawing was loaded new method db_drawing::check() is called. 
		It iterates through tables, entities and objects. For each element 
		of drawing virtual method db_handitem::check(db_drawing*) is called. 
		It is up to particular element how to check and validate itself. 
		For example db_dictionary::check(db_drawing*) iterates records and 
		deletes ones which referencing NULL objects.
		The phase is OPTIONAL. The member variable drw_readwrite::m_bCheckOnLoad 
		controls whether checking is performed. By default it initializes to 
		true in constructor.
		The phase INCREASES overall loading time.
Changed files:	
		Source/prj/lib/DRW/Drw.h?rev=1.1.1.1.14.1

File Name:	VS_27112002_1.txt
Date:		27-11-2002
Developer:	Vittalbabu Srinivasan
Company:	Mantra Software
Reference:	

New files:	
		None

Changed files: 	
		Source/prj/lib/db/handtable.h
		Source/prj/lib/db/handtable.cpp
                Source/prj/lib/db/objhandle.h
                Source/prj/lib/db/objhandle.cpp
 
Deleted files:	
		None

Description:	Reworked fix made for performance improvement in HandleTable::Find().
Comments:	This submission redoes the fix made in VS_02092002_1.txt for HandleTable::Find(),
		The old fix used db_objhandle as a key into an STL map storing db_handitem records.
		Using a class as a key was not a good choice -- the destructor was called on the 
		class on each access. The fix was to create an __int64 representation of the handle
		and use this as a key.


File by File:	
		Source/prj/lib/db/handtable.h			Version: 1.1.1.1.14.4
			Modified m_map to be a map of __int64, db_handitem.
		Source/prj/lib/db/handtable.cpp			Version:1.2.6.3
			In Add and Find, call method to the hanlde's ToHugeInt method and pass this to 
			the map methods.
                Source/prj/lib/db/objhandle.h                         Version:1.1.1.1.14.1
                        Added declaration of new method ToHugeInt() which returns an __int64 representaion of
			the handle.
                Source/prj/lib/db/objhandle.cpp                         Version:1.1.1.1.14.1
                        Added code for new method ToHugeInt() which returns an __int64 representaion of
			the handle.

Date:		27-11-2002
Developer:	Vladimir Vinogradov
Company:	BricsCad
Reference:	
Affected files:	Source/prj/lib/DB/drawing.h
		Source/prj/lib/GR/dispobjs.cpp
Description:	added getNextTabRec and setNextTabRec functions for tables
		This is useful to retain pointer because tblnext can get upset when entmod is used during traversal. 
		The new functions are used in ApplyLayerStatesToXref, because looping function sds_tblnext 
		failed when layers are changed and drawing has xrefs. This caused intellicad to hang.
		also icad explorer failed to freeze layers in xrefs for some drawings 
		because of case sensitive comparison of layernames.

Description:	"long" data type for TOOLBARID had reached its limits. So it was NOT possible to add new hardcoded toolbars to IntelliCAD. Now we have used new #define  long_double __int64 for TOOLBAR ID. In future one can implement the class long_double and have operator & overloaded and keep the current design of toolbar intact. Other option is to change the current implementation of toolbar for tool id.

Date:		21-11-2002
Developer:	Stephen Hou
Company:	Nd Space
Reference:	Sub doc SH_21112002.txt
Changed files:	
		Source/Prj/Lib/CMDS/CmdExtrude.cpp
		Source/Prj/Lib/CMDS/CmdRevolve.cpp
		Source/Prj/Lib/DB/DbAcisEntityData.cpp
		Source/Prj/Lib/DB/DbAcisEntityData.h
		Source/Prj/Lib/DB/Modeler.cpp
		Source/Prj/Lib/ICADLIB/allocator.cpp
		Source/Prj/ICAD/binchange.cpp
		Source/Prj/ICAD/binchange.h
		Source/Prj/ICAD/Change.cpp
		Source/Prj/ICAD/icadapi.cpp
Description:	This submission fixes BugZilla:78359, BugZilla:78355, BugZilla:78364, and BugZilla:78357. 
		and some memory leaks.
Comments:	BugZilla:78359 - Full ACIS-ICAD crashes on cancelling chamfer command

                RESOLUTION: It crashed because the implementation for UNDO for solid 
                            operations was based on wrong assumption that data size 
                            will not change after an operation. This is fixed by 
                            re-implementing UNDO functions.
                BugZilla:78355 - (Full ACIS)-Moving a newly created solid using grips 
                              moves the entity multiple times.
                RESOLUTION: The reason that solids were moved multi-times distance 
                            because it was implemented to take an action for each 
                            grip point. This is incorrect for selecting a grip point 
                            to move solid. This is fixed.
                BugZilla:78364 - Full Acis - Extrude does not work
                BugZilla:78357 - (ACIS) Revolve command does not work.
                RESOLUTION: They didn't work because they were not implemented for
                            LINE,ARC,ELLIPSE,CIRCLE,POLYLINE,LWPOLYLINE,SPLINE. The
                            implementation for those entities has been added.

		Eng-us/versioninfo.rc2?rev=1.1.2.1 
Description:	dll's have versioninfo that is visible in windows explorer(rightclick the dll)
		this versioninfo was never up to date. Parameters in rc files are difficult to use because they
		get replaced by their values as soon as you edit in VC. 
		So the versioninfo was moved to a new file versioninfo.rc2 that is included in the rc files 
		and that does not need editing the parameters are all gathered and edited in the blddate.h file 
		dll specific defines are set in the rc files including versioninfo.rc2 
Comments:	There can be elusive compile problems with the paths. 
		Tricks that can help: in settings/resource paths change backslash in slash, add a './' before the path, 
		and strangely, change case of the path to lowercase (!)

Date:		10-11-2002
Developer:	Stephen Hou
Company:	Nd Space
Reference:	SH_10112002_1.txt

Affected files:		
	Source/Prj/Iacad/IacadView.cpp: 		
	Source/Prj/Lib/cmd/HideAndShade.cpp: 

Description:	This submission fix the bug# 78353.

Comments:       This problem is introduced after I made changes to OnPaint()
                to comment out _USE_OPENGL_ in order to force the hidden line image 
                to be redrawed whenever screen size is changed/hidden. But the 
                change caused the screen to be re-painted every time when the image was
                wireframe, which confused display engine when it drawed dragging 
                objects. To fix the problem, instead of redraw hidden line image, 
                I change the HIDE/SHADE functions to copy the screen DC to off-screen 
                windows' DC after using OpenGL to generate hidden line image.

File Name:	VS_05102002_1.txt
Date:		05-10-2002
Developer:	Vittalbabu Srinivasan
Company:	Mantra Software
Reference:	
Changed files: 	
		Source/prj/lib/DB/reactor.cpp
Description:	Fixed crash when entity with a reactor is deleted.
Comments:	This submission fixes a serious problem in ReactorSubject::BreakAssociation(). The ReactorSubject class has
		an STL list (m_reactors) that stores ReactorItems. In BreakAssociation(), an STL iterator iterates through all elements in
		the list. If the handitem is present it calls BreakAssociation() which through other calls ends up calling
		ReactorSubject::DetachReactor(). Now DetachReactor() ends up removing the current element being processed by
		BreakAssociation(). This leaves the iterator in BreakAssociation() in an invalid state -- we end up looking at 
		memory that was just freed which leads to a crash.

		I have fixed this by a kludge -- before BreakAssociation() is called, I store what the iterator's next position and
		use this for the loop iterator instead of incrementing the iterator after the call to BreakAssociation(). The bigger issue is this is a
		big design flaw -- if a list is being processed, a function being called in this processing loop shouldn't destroy 
		the list. If that is the expected behavior then something other than an STL list must be used to store the elements.
		The outer loop has to be written in a proper manner to handle this and STL list is not the right structure.
		
File by File:	
		Source/prj/lib/DB/reactor.cpp			Version: 
			In ReactorSubject::BreakAssociation() added another LIST_ITER instance. This stores what the iterator's next
			position and is used in the for loop.

Date:		06-09-2002

Changed files: 	
		Source/prj/lib/drw/dwgload.cpp?rev=1.48.4.2
		Source/prj/lib/db/handtable.h?rev=1.1.1.1.14.2
Description:	Performance improvement in load of groups.
Comments:	This submission improves performance of groups in large drawings by a substantial factor. The fix is not to call 
		CDbGroup::addEntity() for each entity in a group in drw_readwrite::drw_marcompopen(). 
		Instead, the linked list is
		maintained and CDbGroup::setEntitiesList() is called. 
		In one large 12MB dwg file, open time came down to 25 sec. from 11 minutes.
		Fixed memory leak in HandleTable class. Added a destructor and cleared the map.
		Removed call to	CDbGroup::addEntity() for each entity in a group in drw_readwrite::drw_marcompopen(). 			Instead, the linked list is
		maintained and CDbGroup::setEntitiesList() is called. 
		Added a destructor which calls clear on the map.

Date:		02-09-2002
Developer:	Vittalbabu Srinivasan
Company:	Mantra Software
Reference:	VS_02092002_1.txt
Changed files: 	
		Source/prj/lib/db/handtable.h
		Source/prj/lib/db/handtable.cpp
                Source/prj/make/db.dsp
Description:	Performance improvement in HandleTable::Find().
Comments:	This submission improves performance of HandleTable::Find() by 2X. 
		The improvement is present when there are
		a large number of handles and HandleTable::Find() is called a lot of times. 
		This happens when dwg files are opened and 
		CIcadDoc::OnOpenDocument() calls drw_openfile() 
		which ends up calling drw_makeeentlist(0 which calls db_drawing_handent()
		which calls HandleTable::Find(). 
		The problem is ICAD is adding entries to a list, sorts the list (via qsort) and then
		does a search on this list. When this loop is repeated a lot of times qsort becomes extremely slow. 			qsort behaves very poorly when sorting a nearly sorted list.
		As an example, drawing demo_.dwg, makes ~7000 calls to HandleTable::Find(). 
		This triggers (through the qsort function) more than 5Billion calls to the compare function. 
		Open of this dwg file is slow.
		The fix is to use an STL map to store the db_handitem and db_objhandle relationship. 
		This improves load time of demo_dwg
		by 200% -- the new code takes 1/3 of the time to load the demo_.dwg file as the old code.
File by File:	
		Source/prj/lib/db/handtable.h
			Replaced HandleArray with a Handle_MAP m_map instance. Added a new typedef for Handle_MAP (which is a STL map) and added a compare
			function for the key (db_objhandle).
		Source/prj/lib/db/handtable.cpp
			In handTable.Add9), the new value is added to m_map. In Find() this is queried to get the value for the key.
                Source/prj/make/db.dsp
                        Removed treat warnings as errors. I cannot suppress Microst C4768 warnings even with a pragma.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Description:	Fixed crash in sds_menucmd() call.
Comments:	The string passed in a sds_menucmd() call can be on the local stack. IcadMenu::DoMenuRef() was
		modifying this string which causes a crash. Fixed this by creating a local copy of the string which
		can be safely modified. The fix is made to the calling function CMainWindow::IcadWndAction

File Name:	VS_21072002_1.txt
Date:		21-07-2002
Developer:	Vittalbabu Srinivasan
Company:	Mantra Software
Reference:	

Affected files: 	
		Source/Regress_apps/regress_dwg_dxf/reg.frx
		Source/Regress_apps/roundtrip_dwg_dxf/reg.frm
		Source/Regress_apps/roundtrip_dwg_dxf/Module1.bas
		Source/Regress_apps/roundtrip_dwg_dxf/roundtrip_dwg_dxf.exe

Description:	Enhancements to Roundtrip application to test dwg and dxf operations between Icad and Acad.
Comments:	The roundtrip_dwg_dxf application allows users to perform roundtrip testing of Icad and Acad and
		to use dwg or dxf as the input for any step. The base applciation does a dxfin or open on the input
		(depending on whether the previous step did a dxfout or save) followed by a dxfout or saveas (depending
		on what the user chose). The output of one step in the input for the next step and upto five steps
		can be specified. FOr each step, Icad or Acad can be chosen and different versions of the executables can be
		chosen for each step.

		The application has been enhanced with the following changes :-

		1. User can now specify additional commands to run in each step. For example, "zoom e " can be  typed into
		the textbox for additional script commands and the application will add this command for each file it processes.
		More than one command can be given as input (eg) 
		zoom, e,erase,all,undo.These commands will be run for all scripts.

		2. User can specify the max. time a script can take to run. If a script hangs due to invalid command, it will be
		automatically terminated after this interval has passed.
		3. Better reporting of results and errors.


File by File:	
		Source/Regress_apps/regress_dwg_dxf/reg.frx		Rev 1.2
		Source/Regress_apps/roundtrip_dwg_dxf/reg.frm		Rev 1.2
			Added 2 textboxes for script timeout intreval and user defined commands for script.
		Source/Regress_apps/roundtrip_dwg_dxf/Module1.bas	Rev 1.2

			and user defined limit for a script.
		Source/Regress_apps/roundtrip_dwg_dxf/roundtrip_dwg_dxf.exe	Rev 1.2
			Updated version of exe

Description:	Roundtrip application to test dwg and dxf operations between Icad and Acad.
Comments:	This roundtrip application allows users to test different versions of Icad and Acad
		for roundtrip compatibility. This allows an user to select Icad or Acad for any step,
		choose different executables for each step (Icad 2001, ACAD R14, etc.), decide on the
		either dxf or dwg as output format. In addition the version to either do a dxfout or
		saveas can be chosen. The output of one step in the input to the next step and a 
		maximum of five steps can be chosen.

		of regress_scr.exe. The user can now choose the ICAD executable to run regress with as well as the
		location of the directory where the scripts are present. 

		This executable has a timer to kill ICAD if it takes more than 5 minutes to run. To change this intreval,
		go to Option->Set to change the intreval. The fact that the scr was killed is logged to the log file.

		This application logs the kernel and user time spent in running the script as well as memory used by the
		application.

File by File:

			Project file.
		CvsHist:Source/Regress_apps/Regress Script application/reg.frm

			well as code to kill long running scripts. Memory and time logging is also performed by this
			module.
		CvsHist:Source/Regress_apps/Regress Script application/Global.bas

		Source/Regress_apps/Roundtrip%20application/roundtrip.vbp

		Source/Regress_apps/Roundtrip%20application/FormHelp.frm 
Affected files:	
		Source/prj/ICAD/icadmain.cpp
Description:	This submission adds a flexible roundtrip application.
		This can be customised to run any combination of ICAD and ACAD versions 
		and to open/save different versions of the dwg file. 
		The restriction is at most 5 steps can be performed. 
		This application is written in Visual Basic and the executable is checked in.
Comments:	
		You would need roundtrip.exe and the 3 bmp files to run the application. 
		The other files are checked in in case someone wants to modify the application.

		This application allows the user to perform roundtrip 
		testing of Icad and Acad. The application allows the user 
		to test from 1 to 5 steps in roundtrip. For each step, either Icad or Acad 
		can be used. In addition, a different version of the executable
		can be used at each step.

		WARNING -- the output directory should not be under the 
		directory to process

		There are two tabs in the application. In the options tab, 
		the user can specify a default location for icad.exe and acad.exe.
		The user can set the directory to process and a directory to 
		place the output files. All dwg files in the input directory are processed
		and the output files placed in the output directory. The input folder 
		is recursively processed and the same hierarchy is created for the output 
		folder.

		The output dwg file from one step in the input dwg file for the next
		step. The appliation builds a scr file on the fly for each dwg file 
		it is processing and for each step. This scr file is run against the
		executable chosen for that step.

		It is the responsibility of the user to ensure that the roundtrip steps
		are valid. For example, if step 1 is ICAD 2001 version and step 2 is ACAD R14 
		version, the saveas for step 1 should be a version ACAD R14 can recognise.
		Also the saveas from step 2 should be a format ACAD R14
		can write out to.

File by File:	
		Source/Regress_apps/Roundtrip%20application/roundtrip.vbp 
			VB project file to build application.
		Source/Regress_apps/Roundtrip%20application/roundtrip.frx 
			Generated VB file.
		Source/Regress_apps/Roundtrip%20application/roundtrip.frm 
			Main form for roundtrip application.
		Source/Regress_apps/Roundtrip%20application/roundtrip.exe 
			Executable for roundtrip.
		Source/Regress_apps/Roundtrip%20application/icadsplashtd.bmp 
			Bitmap for splash screen.
		Source/Regress_apps/Roundtrip%20application/icadsplashOld.bmp 
			Bitmap for splash screen.
		Source/Regress_apps/Roundtrip%20application/icadsplash.bmp

Comments:	This submission adds new functionality to the regress applications. regress_scr.exe automatically
		runs all scr files in a sub-directory called scripts and places its output in output_dxf, log and results
		sub-directories. Now it can take an optional parameter which is the sub-directory where the scripts are present
		The only restriction is this sub-directory cannot be called mem, time, cov or purify. The logfile will now
		have the directory from which the scripts are run as part of its name.
		regress_scr -- runs all scr files in scripts directory. Log file is icadregress_scripts.log
		regress_scr scripts_qa -- runs all scr files in scripts_qa directory. Log file is icadregress_scripts_qa.log
		Some of the scr files which take long to run are moved to scripts_qa directory in regress.
		I have updated regress_acad_icad_roundtrip.exe to run with AutoCAD 2002. The syntax change is for the saveas
		format and it now saves as 2000 (as opposed to A2K in the old code.)

Date:		27-04-2002
Developer:	Vittalbabu Srinivasan
Company:	Mantra Software
Reference:	VS_4272002_1.txt
Changed files:	
		Source/prj/lib/DRW/dwgload.cpp
		Source/prj/lib/SDS/sds_findfile.cpp
Description:	This submission fixes some memory bugs in ICAD. This is an array bounds write bug.
Comments:	A bug which I uncovered in VS_4112002_1.txt has to be fixed in more places. The problem is
		ic_findinpath() makes a call to SearchPath() and this assumes that the size of buffer being
		passed in is 2049. In most cases the buffer we pass in is smaller. I added an argument to
		ic_findinpath() which is the buffer size. I made it a default argument so current code will
		work as is and I made fixes to some functions calling ic_findinpath(). 
		The problem is one of the functions calling ic_findinpath() is sds_findfile(). sds_findfile()
		just calls ic_findinpath(). There are 100+ calls to sds_findfile() in our code. And I could
		not change sds_findfile() to take an argument of bufferSize due to the following problem noted 
		by lint. If I added an  default argument to api\sds\sds.h, ICAD doesn't link any more. Plus a
		bigger reason was the comment that this is an SDS External API -- We can't change API functions
		without discussing this further.
..\lib\SDS\sds_findfile.cpp(300) : Error 1065: Symbol 'sds_findfile(const char
    *, char *)' not declared as "C" conflicts with line 479, file
    ..\api\sds\sds.h
// *****************************************
// This is an SDS External API
//
// SPECIAL !!!
// Because of multiple dependencies, there is no sdsengine_ version
// of this function
//
int 
sds_findfile(const char *szLookFor, char *szPathFound) 
	{
	return ic_findinpath( NULL, szLookFor, szPathFound);
	}
    
	My fix was to replace calls to sds_findfile() by ic_findinpath() as the code above shows it is not a problem. I
	changed the code in the files where I had seen there was a problem (when I opened a dwg file). I did this in 2 files
	sds_findfile.cpp and dwgload.cpp

File Name:	VS_4252002_1.txt
Date:		25-04-2002
Developer:	Vittalbabu Srinivasan
Company:	Mantra Software
Reference:	

Added Files:	
		Source/Regress_apps/Benchmark_icad_14/regress.cpp
		Source/Regress_apps/Benchmark_icad_14/regress.h
		Source/Regress_apps/Benchmark_icad_14/regress_benchmark.dsp
		Source/Regress_apps/Benchmark_icad_14/StdAfx.h
		Source/Regress_apps/Benchmark_icad_14/StdAfx.cpp
		Source/Regress_apps/Benchmark_icad_14/Debug/regress_icad_acad_bench.exe
Description:	This submission adds the source for regress_icad_acad_bench application.
Comments:	This regress application benchmarks icad and acad for 2 cases -- open of dwg files and open followed by save of
		dwg files. If the third argument is set to 0, the benchmark performs open of dwg files only. Setting it to 1
		performs open and save.

		Usage is 

		regress_icad_acad_bench "Directory_to_process" "Output_Directory" 0

		The benchmark executable process all dwg files in the "Directory_to_process". It recurses to find all
		dwg files in the hierarchy and processes them. It writes the output files in the same directory structure
		under "Output_Directory". 

		It is IMPORTANT that "Output_Directory" be not present under "Directory_to_process". If it is, the processing
		will never end.

		The regress_icad_acad_bench executable saves dwg files and dxf files with the same prefix as the dwg
		file it is processing. For each directory under "Directory_to_process" it processes, it creates 2 directories 
		output_R14 and output_acad_R14. The saved dwg files (if optin is set to 1) are placed here.

		Required system variables :-

		ICAD_REGRESS_EXE_PATH -- This has the complete path (including icad.exe) to the icad executable.
		ACAD_REGRESS_EXE_PATH -- This has the complete path (including acad.exe) to the acad executable.
		The following are optional --
		TT_EXE -- True Time executable
		ICAD_TT_REGRESS_EXE_PATH -- ICAD executable instrumented with TrueTime.
		BC_EXE -- Boundschecker executable.
		TC_EXE -- Truecoverage executable.
		ICAD_COV_REGRESS_EXE_PATH -- ICAD executable instrumented with TrueCoverage.
		PURIFY_EXE -- Purify executable.
		ICAD_PURIFY_EXE -- Icad executable instrumented by Purify.

		Output file :-

		c:/icadregress.log



File by File:	
		Source/Regress_apps/Benchmark_icad_14/regress.cpp
			
			This file contains the source for the regress_scr application.

		Source/Regress_apps/Benchmark_icad_14/regress.h
			This header file pulls in MFC structures like CString.
		Source/Regress_apps/Benchmark_icad_14/regress_benchmark.dsp
			This is the project file for regress.
		Source/Regress_apps/Benchmark_icad_14/StdAfx.h
			This is a placeholder. Nothing much is in here.
		Source/Regress_apps/Benchmark_icad_14/StdAfx.cpp
		This is a placeholder for future code.
	Source/Regress_apps/Benchmark_icad_14/Debug/regress_icad_acad_bench.exe

			The benchmark executable.

Description:	This submission fixes a bug from my last submission in table.cpp. Fixed lint problem in same file.
Comments:	This submission fixes a bug in LISP\table.cpp. A resbuf was previously being deleted which I changed to a
		sds_relrb(). I need to set the rbnext pointer of this resbuf to NULL -- or else it will free buffers which
		it should not. This was fixed in lsp_modify_adslist().
		Also fixed a lint warning in table.cpp -- In function lsp_tblobjname() removed a local variable (rb) 
		which was set but not used.

File by File:

Reference:	EBA_4242002_2.txt
Added files:
Affected files: 
Description:
Comments:
	Automation Enhancement about SHAPE object.

	Shape Object
			IntelliCAD SHAPE Entity.
		Object Specific Methods
			None
		Common Object Methods
			Same as other Entity Object.
			(ex. Copy, Rotate, Update ...)
		Object Specific Properties
			InsertionPoint As Point
				SHAPE Insertion Point (DXF=10)
			Name As String
				SHAPE name (DXF=3)
			Normal As Vector
				Extrusion Direction vector (DXF=210)
			Rotation As Double
				Rotation angle (DXF=50)
			Height As Double
				SHAPE height (DXF=40)
			ScaleFactor As Double
				SHAPE Width factor (DXF=41)
			ObliqueAngle As Double
				SHAPE Oblique angle (DXF=51)
			Thickness As Double
				SHAPE Thickness (DXF=39)
		Common Object Properties
			Same as other Entity Object.
			(ex. Layer, Color, Visible ...)

	TextStyle Object New Property
		Shape As Boolean
			True: This is STYLE for SHAPE.
			False: This is STYLE for TEXT.
			(DXF=70, bit0)

	Document Object New Method
		Sub LoadShapeFile( Filename As String )
			Load shape file to use SHAPE object.
			Filename can set with/without path.

	ModelSpace, PaperSpace, BlockRecord Object New Method
		Function AddShape( Name As String, InsertionPoint As Point, 
			Height As Double, Rotation As Rotation) As Shape
			Adds a Shape entity with given height and rotation
			Height and Rotation are optional arguments.

	Automation Enhancement about GetLispVariable/SetLispVariable.
		Automation		Lisp
		-------------------------
		VARIANT_TRUE	RTT
		VARIANT_FALSE	RTNIL

Date:		21-04-2002
Developer:	Vittalbabu Srinivasan
Company:	Mantra Software
Reference:	VS_4212002_4.txt
Affected files:	
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/pedit2.cpp
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/offset.cpp
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/dimension.cpp
		Source/prj/lib/LISP/table.cpp
		Source/prj/lib/LISP/system.cpp
		Source/prj/lib/LISP/interpreter.cpp
		Source/prj/lib/LISP/freers.cpp
Description:	This submission fixes infinte loop, memory leaks, memory problems and bugs in ICAD.
Comments:	This submission fixes infinite loop, memory problems and bugs in ICAD.
		These errors were found when I ran Purify with the new scr files I added to
		regress. I identified an infinte loop in pedit and multiple types of memory
		bugs. The memory bugs were mismatched memory operations -- memory allocated in new
		and deallocated in free and memory allocated by malloc and deallocated by delete.
		Then there were cases of reading freed memory, deallocating memory twice, freeing
		invalid memory (literally freeing a random address) and array bound read/write.

		These type of memory problems are serious as ICAD would crash unpredictably. There are
		still more cases of memory errors which I need to fix -- these are uninitialised memory reads.

		In pedit, if all the vertices of the polyline we select to edit are outside the window, the
		code in function cmd_pline_editvtx() goes into an infinte loop. The code (in 3 places) tries to
		find a start vertex for the polyline which lies inside the boundary. It calls function nextvert()
		but this function loops around to the start vertex if it reaches the end. Result was an infinite loop.
		The fix was to select the first vertex if this occured.
		Fixed a crash in trim_or_extend(). An index to array onLocal1 was uninitilised. The behavior was
		unpredicatble and causes crashes. Fixed this by setting the index to 0.
		Fixed memory mismatch in cmd_doverride(). We were leaking memory when a locally allocated resbuf was
		not freed. Also memory allocated by malloc wes being deallocated by delete. free() is now called instead.
		Fixed bugs in lsp_modify_adslist(). In this function we were deleting a pointer to a locally allocated resbuf
		instead of calling sds_relrb()> Changed the code to call sds_relrb().
		FIxed a memory mismatch in lsp_getvar(). Here a loccally allocated resbuf gets a string through malloc which
		was being deallocated by delete. Changed this to free() after veryfing all paths through the code allocated
		the string by malloc().
		In lsp_1associtem() if the source resbuf holds a string which happens to be empty, the function was trying 
		to allocate a string by looking at the strlen() of this string. This causes crashes. Fixed this by setting the
		result resbuf to an empty string if source string was empty.
		A wide range of bugs came due to bugs in lsp_freesuprb() and lsp_freesplrb(). Here resbufs strings and binary
		data were deallocated but the pointers were not set to NULL. This caused memory to be freed twice, freed memory being 
		read, etc.

Date:		21-04-2002
Developer:	Vittalbabu Srinivasan
Company:	Mantra Software
Reference:	VS_4212002_2.txt
Added files:	
		Source/Regress_apps/Regress_icad_14/regress.cpp
		Source/Regress_apps/Regress_icad_14/regress.h
		Source/Regress_apps/Regress_icad_14/regress_roundtrip.dsp
		Source/Regress_apps/Regress_icad_14/StdAfx.h
		Source/Regress_apps/Regress_icad_14/StdAfx.cpp
Description:	This submission adds the source for regress_icad_acad_roundtrip application.
Comments:	There are two regress applications. The second regress application performs a roundtrip between
		ICAD and ACAD. Here we open a dwg file in ICAD, save it as dwg, open the dwg file in ACAD, save it
		as dwg and reopen the file saved by ACAD in ICAD. The roundtrip is currently tested against ACAD R14 
		and to get it run against ACAD 2000/2002 would require slight change to the source. This change is the 
		prompt which ACAD uses in the save command. This is done by creating scr files on the fly to open the dwg file
		save in the formats shown below and quit and running the scripts.
		Usage is 
		regress_icad_acad_roundtrip "Directory_to_process" "Output_Directory"
		The roundtrip executable process all dwg files in the "Directory_to_process". It recurses to find all
		dwg files in the hierarchy and processes them. It writes the output files in the same directory structure
		under "Output_Directory". 
		It is IMPORTANT that "Output_Directory" be not present under "Directory_to_process". If it is, the processing
		will never end.
		The regress_icad_acad_roundtrip executable saves multiple dwg files and dxf files with the same prefix as the dwg
		file it is processing. For each directory under "Directory_to_process" it processes, it creates 12 directories
		For the first ICAD operation on a dwg file, it will save dwg files in 3 formats and a dxf file.
		output_2k, output_LT95 and output_R14 have the dwg file saved in 2K, LT95 and R14 formats.
		output_dxf has the dxf file.
		If we are testing roundtrip against R14, then ACAD will open the saved file in output_R14 directory. It will
		in turn write 2 dwg files and 1 dxf file.
		output_acad_LT95 and output_acad_R14 have the dwg file saved in LT95 and R14 formats.
		output_acad_dxf has the dxf file.
		If we were doing a roundtrip against ACAD 2K, then a dwg file will be written to output_acad_2k directory.
		Finally ICAD will open the dwg file saved by ACAD R14 in the output_R14 directory and save 3 dwg and 1 dxf
		file.
		output_round_2k, output_round_LT95 and output_round_R14 have the dwg file saved in 2K, LT95 and R14 formats.
		output_round_dxf has the dxf file.
		This structure opens up the possibilities for stress testing roundtrip which is not coded yet. We could make 
		ICAD open the files written by ACAD in LT95 format or have ACAD open the LT95 format and have the second run of
		ICAD open the 2K version. We could also do dxfin on the various formats.
		Required system variables :-
		ICAD_REGRESS_EXE_PATH -- This has the complete path (including icad.exe) to the icad executable.
		ACAD_REGRESS_EXE_PATH -- This has the complete path (including acad.exe) to the acad executable.
		ACAD_REGRESS_VER -- This tells the applciation wheich version of the saved dwg file ACAD will open.
				    This is also used by the second run of ICAD.
		The following are optional --
		TT_EXE -- True Time executable
		ICAD_TT_REGRESS_EXE_PATH -- ICAD executable instrumented with TrueTime.
		BC_EXE -- Boundschecker executable.
		TC_EXE -- Truecoverage executable.
		ICAD_COV_REGRESS_EXE_PATH -- ICAD executable instrumented with TrueCoverage.
		PURIFY_EXE -- Purify executable.
		ICAD_PURIFY_EXE -- Icad executable instrumented by Purify.
		Output file :-
		c:/icadregress.log

Reference:	VS_4212002_1.txt
Added files:	
		Source/Regress_apps/Regress_scr/regress.cpp
		Source/Regress_apps/Regress_scr/regress.h
		Source/Regress_apps/Regress_scr/regress_scr.dsp
		Source/Regress_apps/Regress_scr/StdAfx.h
		Source/Regress_apps/Regress_scr/StdAfx.cpp
Description:	This submission adds the source for regress_scr application.
Comments:	There are two regress applications. The first regress application runs the regress suite
		consisting of scr files. The executable (regress_scr.exe) is placed in the Regress directory.
		Under the Regress directory are the following directories :-
		scripts -- this directory stored the scr files to run regress. Each scr file will load lsp files and/or
			   run commands directly. The last steps in the scr file are to write out a dxf file with the same
			   prefix name as the scr file in the output_dxf directory follwed by a quit command. This way each
			   scr file will automatically exit.
		LISP -- this directory and its child directories stores LSP files which the scr files load and run.
			Since the scr files are run from the parent directory (which is Regress), scr files should do
			(load "Regress/aaa.lsp") to load aaa.lsp file.
		output_dxf -- Each scr file will write a dxf file to this directory.
		base -- The base dxf files for comparison are placed here.
		results -- The regress_scr can run Purify, Boundschecker, TrueTime and TrueCoverage builds. The output
			   files from these progra,s are placed here.
		log -- Each scr file will write a log file saved to this directory. This facility doesn't work properly.
		Required system variables :-
		ICAD_REGRESS_EXE_PATH -- This has the complete path (including icad.exe) to the icad executable.
		The following are optional --
		TT_EXE -- True Time executable
		ICAD_TT_REGRESS_EXE_PATH -- ICAD executable instrumented with TrueTime.
		BC_EXE -- Boundschecker executable.
		TC_EXE -- Truecoverage executable.
		ICAD_COV_REGRESS_EXE_PATH -- ICAD executable instrumented with TrueCoverage.
		PURIFY_EXE -- Purify executable.
		ICAD_PURIFY_EXE -- Icad executable instrumented by Purify.
		Output file :-
		icadregress.log		
		The regress_scr.exe processes all scr files in the scripts directory. After the scr file completes, it modifies
		some of the output lines in the dxf file written out to the output_dxf directory to set variables like 
		TD_CREATE, $TDUPDATE, $TDINDWG and $TDUSRTIMER to 0.0. Then this dxf file is compared to a base dxf file and 
		differences (if any) are logged to a log file. The log file also has the time spent in running each scr file and 
		the total time spent to run regress.

File Name:	VS_3252002_1.txt
Date:		25-03-2002
Developer:	Vittalbabu Srinivasan
Company:	Mantra Software
Reference:	
Changed files:	
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/cmds4.cpp
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/cmdssDimVars.cpp
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/dimensions.cpp
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/DimStyle.cpp
Description:	This submission fixes memory problems in dimension portion of ICAD.
Comments:	This submission fixes memory problems identified when I ran Boundschecker against
		dimensioning scripts created by Cybage. There are two types of error -- one was writing
		beyond the bounds of an array and the second was mismatch of malloc/calloc/free and new/delete
		calls.
		Writing beyond the array bounds occured when a new string is created to keep a copy of an existing
		string but the allocation fails to allocate an extra space to store the trailing EOS character.
		Memory mismatches occur when memory is allocated by malloc or calloc and freed by delete and memory allocated
		by new freed by a call to free. This leads to undefined behavior.
		For these scripts, I created the base file by running against the current source and compared them against
		the results after the change. One script file (DimUpdateAll.scr) shows some differences. Cybage QA 
		should look at this.



File by File:	
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/cmds4.cpp 			New Rev. 1.20
			Fixed memory mismatch. String has to be malloced as it is freed later.		
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/cmdssDimVars.cpp		New Rev. 1.9
			This file has a structure plinkvar which for string system variables stores the sysvar information.
			This buffer comes from SDS_getvar() which calls malloc and other calls in the file change this buffer.
			The change functionality uses new and we have a big mismatch. What call do you use to free this buffer
			delete or free? In some cases the buffer was allocated by malloc and in some cases the same buffer
			was reallocated using new. Given the large number of calls to new to set plinkvar, I did not change 
			them. Instead, I changed the initial set of these buffers by using new. A new function copyStrToPlinkVar()
			copies the resbuf values to a new buffer allocated by new and frees the resbuf buffer.
			did the same for layername though this variable is present as an extern in multiple files.
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/dimensions.cpp 		New Rev. 1.34
			In cmd_doverride(), buffer allocated by new has to be released by call to delete.
		Source/prj/lib/CMDS/DimStyle.cpp		New Rev. 1.5
			layername is an extern char* variable declared in cmdDimVars.cpp This memory location is released
			by a call to delete and we have to call new when setting a value in cmd_DimStyleFunc(). 
			The buffer allocated to store the layername and DB_QCLAYER should have an extra character to store
			trailing EOS.

Description:	This submission updates regress suite to IntelliCAD.
Comments:	The regress suite has been updated. Instead of a batch file, an executable (regress_scr.exe) is present.
		The regress_scr.exe automatically runs all scr files in the scripts subdirectory.

		The scr files set logfileon and the logfile is written to the log directory. The output dxf file is 
		placed in output_dxf directory and is processed to reset values for $TDCREATE, $TDUPDATE, $TDINDWG and
		$TDUSRTIMER to 0.0. The base dxf files have these values set to 0.0. The output dxf file and base dxf file are 
		compared and differences (if any) are written to the icadregress.log file.

		Another change -- the base files will no longer have a suffix of base in the file name (ie) the base file for 
		arctex_at.scr will not be arctex_at_base.dxf but arctex_at.dxf.
File by File:	Source/regress/log
			New directory. Log files will be written here.
		Source/regress/output_dxf
			New directory. dxf files will be written here.
		Source/regress/scripts/3dspiral_3dspiral.scr
			logfile is turned on.
		Source/regress/base/3dspiral_3dspiral_base.dxf
			logfile is turned on.
		Source/regress/scripts/3dspiral_spiral.scr
			logfile is turned on.
		Source/regress/base/3dspiral_spiral.dxf
			Base dxf file for 3dspiral_spiral test case. $TDCREATE, $TDUPDATE, $TDINDWG and
			$TDUSRTIMER to 0.0.
		Source/regress/scripts/arctex_at.scr
			logfile is turned on.
		Source/regress/base/arctex_at.dxf

			$TDUSRTIMER to 0.0.

Date:		10-3-2002
Developer:	Vittalbabu Srinivasan
Company:	Mantra Software
Reference:	
Added files:	Source/regress
		Source/regress/modify.xml
		Source/regress/Readme.txt
		Source/regress/regress.bat
		Source/regress/scripts/3dspiral_3dspiral.scr
		Source/regress/scripts/arctex_at.scr
		Source/regress/scripts/3dspiral_spiral.scr
		Source/regress/base/3dspiral_spiral_base.dxf
		Source/regress/base/3dspiral_3dspiral_base.dxf
		Source/regress/base/arctex_at_base.dxf
		Source/regress/LISP
		Source/regress/LISP/3dspiral.lsp
		Source/regress/LISP/ARCTEX.lsp
		Source/regress/sds
Description:	This submission adds a regress suite to IntelliCAD.
Comments:	file VS_3102002_1.txt
		This is the initial version of a regress suite for IntelliCAD. The regress suite consists of
		scr files which are run from a batch file (regress.bat). Base dxf files are provided and each
		scr file is expected to write out a dxf file to comapre with the base file. The output from
		regress is written to regress.log file.
		The Readme.txt file shows what environment variable to set and how to add new tests to the regress suite.
		Currently 3 scr files have been added and more will be added shortly.
		Currently the regress suite will report errors for each of the script files. This is due to the fact 
		the dxf values for $TDCREATE, $TDUPDATE, $TDINDWG and $TDUSRTIMER vary for each run of ICAD. A fix 
		will be made for this shortly.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Date:		11-10-2001
Developer:	Gil Crouse
Company:	DaVinci Technologies, Inc.
Reference:
Affected files:	Source/prj/lib/AUTO/autohelpers.cpp
Description:	Fixed a problem in copying blocks in the routine copyhip.
		The previous code always did a complex copy on the block
		inserts, but blocks are not always complex and so the
		complex copy would copy the block and else on the list
		until it hit a SEQEND or BLOCKEND which was bad.  Blocks
		are only complex when they have attributes.  Changed the
		code so that it only does a complex copy when the block
		has attributes, otherwise just a simple copy.
Comments:

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Date:		11-10-2001
Developer:	Gil Crouse
Company:	DaVinci Technologies, Inc.
Reference:
Affected files:	Source/prj/lib/CMDS/pedit2.cpp
Description:	Fixed a problem with editing a LWPolyline.  If the LWPolyline
		has EED then edititng would fail and would corrupt the points
		of the LWPolyline.  The editing code creates a polyline from
		the lwpolyline before editing it and then converts it back.
		Before if the LWPolyline had EED then the creation of the
		polyline points would fail silently.  This is now fixed.

Comments:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Date:		11-10-2001
Developer:	Gil Crouse
Company:	DaVinci Technologies, Inc.
Reference:
Affected files:	Source/prj/ICAD/ICADMain.cpp
Description:	Fixed problem with XOR color when using a white background
		Before the XOR color was NOT the background color which
		resulted in black for a white background.  But XORing with
		black does nothing so the highlights didn't show up with a
		white background.
		Changed it so it uses a light gray instead

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Date:		09-10-2001 (JP 04-09-2001)
Developer:	Y.Maeda
Company:	SystemMetrix
Reference:
Affected files:
		Source/prj/ICAD/paths.cpp
		Source/prj/ICAD/Preferences.cpp
		Source/prj/ICAD/Preferences.h
		Source/prj/ICAD/IcadApp.cpp
		Source/prj/ICAD/icadcommandlineinfo.cpp
		Source/prj/ICAD/icadcommandlineinfo.h
		Source/prj/lib/AUTO/icadplotcfg.cpp
Description:
		Profile support.
		It added the starting option (/Pxxxx) of ICAD.EXE.
		/P is the option key word of the change profile name.
		xxxx is the string of the profile name.
		If "/P" option isn't set, the 3rd key word becomes "Default".
		If "/P" option is set, the 3rd key word is changed.
		ex) not /P option : ITC/IntelliCAD/Default
		set -PTest    : ITC/IntelliCAD/Test
		set /pMyReg   : ITC/IntelliCAD/MyReg
Comments:	TalJ110091
